        }

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

Platform>WebAppProvider

This is a replacement &amp; improvement on the old implementation based on Extensions.

This is a branching-out of bugs that have previously sat in 
UI>Browser>WebAppInstalls, but are specific to the WebAppProvider infrastructure. This infrastructure lives in chrome/browser/web_applications, and has an aptly-named root class of WebAppProvider.">

I only tested this with explicitly specifying a `--user-data-dir=` because of the comment in [1] about the flag expecting a specific profile dir to be set to avoid the profile picker. It may reproduce without specifying it, but I haven't tested.



<span class="line"><!---->I only tested this with explicitly specifying a `--user-data-dir=` because of the comment in [1] about the flag expecting a specific profile dir to be set to avoid the profile picker. It may reproduce without specifying it, but I haven't tested.<!----></span>

Adding the WebAppProvider component and FoundIn-102 (current Windows Stable).



<span class="line"><!---->Adding the WebAppProvider component and FoundIn-102 (current Windows Stable).<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





For now, I'm setting this as Security_Severity-Medium: this a browser process UAF, but it requires an webapp to be installed and a nonstandard command-line flag to be used to trigger this particular flow. Medium seems reasonable out of an abundance of caution if this might be reachable from the standard "Uninstall" flow under certain conditions.



<span class="line"><!---->For now, I'm setting this as Security_Severity-Medium: this a browser process UAF, but it requires an webapp to be installed and a nonstandard command-line flag to be used to trigger this particular flow. Medium seems reasonable out of an abundance of caution if this might be reachable from the standard "Uninstall" flow under certain conditions.<!----></span>

DPWA: fix UAF on launch --uninstall-app-id



<span class="line"><!---->DPWA: fix UAF on launch --uninstall-app-id<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





`WebAppUninstallDialogDelegateView` is a `DialogDelegate` and is owned by its widget. It was



<span class="line"><!---->`WebAppUninstallDialogDelegateView` is a `DialogDelegate` and is owned by its widget. It was<!----></span>



<br>





triggering a callback on `OnDialogCanceled`.



<span class="line"><!---->triggering a callback on `OnDialogCanceled`.<!----></span>



<br>





The callback was passed from `WebAppUiManagerImpl` to release a



<span class="line"><!---->The callback was passed from `WebAppUiManagerImpl` to release a<!----></span>



<br>





`ScopedKeepAlive`, which could trigger a browser shutdown and further



<span class="line"><!---->`ScopedKeepAlive`, which could trigger a browser shutdown and further<!----></span>



<br>





attempts to close the dialog widget, which races with the widget &



<span class="line"><!---->attempts to close the dialog widget, which races with the widget &amp;<!----></span>



<br>





delegate's destruction managed by views framework.



<span class="line"><!---->delegate's destruction managed by views framework.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





The fix removes the redundant and too-early callback call on



<span class="line"><!---->The fix removes the redundant and too-early callback call on<!----></span>



<br>





`OnDialogCanceled` and only call it on destruction.



<span class="line"><!---->`OnDialogCanceled` and only call it on destruction.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

<a class="strike-through" target="_blank" href="/p/chromium/issues/detail?id=1330289" title="Security: heap-use-after-free in views::DialogDelegate::CancelDialog"><!---->Bug: 1330289<!----></a>

<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.

           * height of the viewport, we want to make sure
           * there's spacing. */

          display: block;
          min-width: 100px;

          overflow: auto;
